\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01447}01447 \textcolor{comment}{    /// where \(\backslash\)f\$ r=\(\backslash\)sqrt\{pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)\} \(\backslash\)f\$. The values of a and b are}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01453}\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1GMRES_ad076ed019b21fa5348e3e65aeba1e27c}{01453}} \textcolor{comment}{}    \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1GMRES_ad076ed019b21fa5348e3e65aeba1e27c}{generate\_plane\_rotation}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dx, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dy, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& cs, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& sn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01454}01454     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01455}01455       \textcolor{comment}{// If dy=0 then we do not need to apply a rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01456}01456       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dy == 0.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01457}01457       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01458}01458         \textcolor{comment}{// Using theta=0 gives cos(theta)=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01459}01459         cs = 1.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01460}01460 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01461}01461         \textcolor{comment}{// Using theta=0 gives sin(theta)=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01462}01462         sn = 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01463}01463       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01464}01464       \textcolor{comment}{// If dx or dy is large using the normal form of calculting cs and sn}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01465}01465       \textcolor{comment}{// is naive since this may overflow or underflow so instead we calculate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01466}01466       \textcolor{comment}{// r=sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)) by using r=|dy|sqrt(1+pow(dx/dy,2)) if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01467}01467       \textcolor{comment}{// |dy|>|dx| [see <A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01468}01468       \textcolor{comment}{// HREF=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypot"{}>Hypot</A>.].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01469}01469       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fabs(dy) > fabs(dx))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01470}01470       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01471}01471         \textcolor{comment}{// Since |dy|>|dx| calculate the ratio dx/dy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01472}01472         \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = dx / dy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01473}01473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01474}01474         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate sin(theta)=dy/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01475}01475         sn = 1.0 / sqrt(1.0 + temp * temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01476}01476 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01477}01477         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate cos(theta)=dx/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))=(dx/dy)*sin(theta)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01478}01478         cs = temp * sn;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01479}01479       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01480}01480       \textcolor{comment}{// Otherwise, we have |dx|>=|dy| so to, again, avoid overflow or underflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01481}01481       \textcolor{comment}{// calculate the values of cs and sn using the method above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01482}01482       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01483}01483       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01484}01484         \textcolor{comment}{// Since |dx|>=|dy| calculate the ratio dy/dx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01485}01485         \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = dy / dx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01486}01486 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01487}01487         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate cos(theta)=dx/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01488}01488         cs = 1.0 / sqrt(1.0 + temp * temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01489}01489 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01490}01490         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate sin(theta)=dy/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))=(dy/dx)*cos(theta)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01491}01491         sn = temp * cs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01492}01492       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01493}01493     \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of generate\_plane\_rotation}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01497}01497 \textcolor{comment}{    /// \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} dx \(\backslash\)newline dy \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)leftarrow \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)newline -\/\(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} dx \(\backslash\)newline dy \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\}. \(\backslash\)f]}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01499}01499     \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01501}01501       \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = cs * dx + sn * dy;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01849}01849         \textcolor{comment}{// to the solution vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01850}01850         \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1AugmentedProblemGMRES_a71199dc59da3f5077803829e36ad4aec}{apply\_schur\_complement\_preconditioner}}(temp, z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01851}01851 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01852}01852         \textcolor{comment}{// Use the update: x\_m=x\_0+inv(M)Vy [see Saad Y,"{}Iterative methods for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01853}01853         \textcolor{comment}{// sparse linear systems"{}, p.284]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01854}01854         x += z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01855}01855       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01856}01856     \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of update}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01857}01857 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01858}01858 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Helper function: Generate a plane rotation. This is done by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01859}01859 \textcolor{comment}{    /// finding the values of \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)cos(\(\backslash\)theta) \(\backslash\)f\$ (i.e. cs) and \(\backslash\)sin(\(\backslash\)theta)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01860}01860 \textcolor{comment}{    /// (i.e. sn) such that:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01861}01861 \textcolor{comment}{    /// \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)newline -\/\(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} dx \(\backslash\)newline dy \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} = \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} r \(\backslash\)newline 0 \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\}, \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01862}01862 \textcolor{comment}{    /// where \(\backslash\)f\$ r=\(\backslash\)sqrt\{pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)\} \(\backslash\)f\$. The values of a and b are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01863}01863 \textcolor{comment}{    /// given by:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01864}01864 \textcolor{comment}{    /// \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta\&=\(\backslash\)dfrac\{dx\}\{\(\backslash\)sqrt\{pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)\}\}, \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01865}01865 \textcolor{comment}{    /// and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01866}01866 \textcolor{comment}{    /// \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta\&=\(\backslash\)dfrac\{dy\}\{\(\backslash\)sqrt\{pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)\}\}. \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01867}01867 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Taken from: Saad Y."{}Iterative methods for sparse linear systems"{}, p.192}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01868}\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1AugmentedProblemGMRES_a74bb2d9ceab6473c1922b166ebf48681}{01868}} \textcolor{comment}{}    \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1AugmentedProblemGMRES_a74bb2d9ceab6473c1922b166ebf48681}{generate\_plane\_rotation}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dx, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dy, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& cs, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& sn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01869}01869     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01870}01870       \textcolor{comment}{// If dy=0 then we do not need to apply a rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01871}01871       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dy == 0.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01872}01872       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01873}01873         \textcolor{comment}{// Using theta=0 gives cos(theta)=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01874}01874         cs = 1.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01875}01875 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01876}01876         \textcolor{comment}{// Using theta=0 gives sin(theta)=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01877}01877         sn = 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01878}01878       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01879}01879       \textcolor{comment}{// If dx or dy is large using the normal form of calculting cs and sn}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01880}01880       \textcolor{comment}{// is naive since this may overflow or underflow so instead we calculate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01881}01881       \textcolor{comment}{// r=sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2)) by using r=|dy|sqrt(1+pow(dx/dy,2)) if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01882}01882       \textcolor{comment}{// |dy|>|dx| [see <A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01883}01883       \textcolor{comment}{// HREF=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypot"{}>Hypot</A>.].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01884}01884       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fabs(dy) > fabs(dx))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01885}01885       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01886}01886         \textcolor{comment}{// Since |dy|>|dx| calculate the ratio dx/dy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01887}01887         \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = dx / dy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01888}01888 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01889}01889         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate sin(theta)=dy/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01890}01890         sn = 1.0 / sqrt(1.0 + temp * temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01891}01891 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01892}01892         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate cos(theta)=dx/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))=(dx/dy)*sin(theta)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01893}01893         cs = temp * sn;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01894}01894       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01895}01895       \textcolor{comment}{// Otherwise, we have |dx|>=|dy| so to, again, avoid overflow or underflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01896}01896       \textcolor{comment}{// calculate the values of cs and sn using the method above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01897}01897       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01898}01898       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01899}01899         \textcolor{comment}{// Since |dx|>=|dy| calculate the ratio dy/dx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01900}01900         \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = dy / dx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01901}01901 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01902}01902         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate cos(theta)=dx/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01903}01903         cs = 1.0 / sqrt(1.0 + temp * temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01904}01904 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01905}01905         \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate sin(theta)=dy/sqrt(pow(dx,2)+pow(dy,2))=(dy/dx)*cos(theta)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01906}01906         sn = temp * cs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01907}01907       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01908}01908     \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of generate\_plane\_rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01909}01909 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01910}01910 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Helper function: Apply plane rotation. This is done using the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01911}01911 \textcolor{comment}{    /// update:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01912}01912 \textcolor{comment}{    /// \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} dx \(\backslash\)newline dy \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)leftarrow \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)newline -\/\(\backslash\)sin\(\backslash\)theta \& \(\backslash\)cos\(\backslash\)theta \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\} \(\backslash\)begin\{bmatrix\} dx \(\backslash\)newline dy \(\backslash\)end\{bmatrix\}. \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01913}\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1AugmentedProblemGMRES_a175361cb4600f20511213636f2e645ce}{01913}} \textcolor{comment}{}    \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1AugmentedProblemGMRES_a175361cb4600f20511213636f2e645ce}{apply\_plane\_rotation}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dx, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& dy, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& cs, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\& sn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01914}01914     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01915}01915       \textcolor{comment}{// Calculate the value of dx but don't update it yet}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01916}01916       \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} temp = cs * dx + sn * dy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01917}01917 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01918}01918       \textcolor{comment}{// Set the value of dy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01919}01919       dy = -\/sn * dx + cs * dy;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{iterative__linear__solver_8h_source_l01922}01922       dx = temp;}
